-- Table structure for table `zip_province_new`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `zip_province_new` (
  `zip_province_id` char(2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `province_id` int(8) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `zip_province_nm_th` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `zip_province_nm_en` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `region_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,

  KEY `province_id` (`province_id`),
  KEY `region_id` (`region_id`),
  KEY `zip_province_id` (`zip_province_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=tis620;

create view   view_province as
SELECT c.zip_tambon_id,c.zip_tambon_nm_th,c.zip_tambon_nm_en,a.zip_amphur_id, a.zip_amphur_nm_th,a.zip_amphur_nm_en, b.zip_province_id, b.zip_province_nm_th, b.zip_province_nm_en,b.province_id,c.zipcode
FROM `zip_amphur_new` AS a
INNER JOIN zip_province_new AS b ON a.zip_province_id = b.zip_province_id

inner join zip_tambon_new as c
on a.zip_amphur_id=c.zip_amphur_id
